      <h2>
       <b>
        \xd0\xa3\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd1\x85 \xd1\x84\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbc \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8!
       </b>
      </h2>

      \n
      <p>
       \xd0\x95\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x89\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82  \xd0\x92\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5  \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8e\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 6 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb8 22 \xd0\x97\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 8 \xd1\x8f\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f 2001 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xe2\x84\x96 372-3 \xc2\xab\xd0\x9e \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8f\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xc2\xbb \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x87\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8  \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe       </p>
      \n\t
     </div>

\xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xc2\xbb\r\n\xd0\xb2 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb2\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8f\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd0\x97\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\r\n\xc2\xab\xd0\x9e \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\r\n\xd0\xb2 \xd0\x97\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xc2\xab\xd0\x9e \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb2 \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9           \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\r\n\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb1 \xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f, \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x88\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd0\x95\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd1\x84\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 (\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x83\xd1\x89\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f)\r\n

\xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 12 \xd1\x84\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f 2013 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xe2\x84\x9626 \xc2\xab\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb1 \xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xc2\xab\xd0\x9e \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb4\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd1\x81\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2 \xd0\x95\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd1\x84\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe-\xd0\xba\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5, \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb8 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd1\x85 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb4\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85 \xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xc2\xbb (\xd0\xa1\xd0\x90\xd0\x97 13-7)

\xd0\xb8 "\xd0\x92\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x87\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x81\xd1\x84\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8f\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f"" (\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x83\xd1\x89\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f)

\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f, \xd0\x9a\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x86, \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e \xd1\x84\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe (\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe) \xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f" (\xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xe2\x84\x96 6954 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 21 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f 2014 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0)(\xd0\xa1\xd0\x90\xd0\x97 14-47)
         </a>

\xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 22 \xd1\x84\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f 2013 \xd0\xb3. \xe2\x84\x9630 \xc2\xab\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb1 \xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f "\xd0\x9e \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb4\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x86\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc, \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\x97\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 11 \xd1\x8f\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f 2010 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xe2\x84\x96 8-\xd0\x97-IV "\xd0\x9e \xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8f \xd1\x83\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8, \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb8 \xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8, \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e\xc2\xbb (\xd0\xa0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xe2\x84\x96 6389 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 19 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f 2013 \xd0\xb3.) (\xd0\xa1\xd0\x90\xd0\x97 13-15)
         </a>
        </td>

\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb5\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\x9f\xd0\x9c\xd0\xa0 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 4 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f 2008 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xe2\x84\x96 786 "\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb1 \xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb4\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f (\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe) == 4) || // \xd0\x94\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\n                    (i == 9 && D.getMonth() == 4) || // \xd0\x94\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\n\n                    (i == 2 && D.getMonth() == 8) || // \xd0\x94\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c \xd0\x9f\xd0\x9c\xd0\xa0\n\n                    (i == 7 && D.getMonth() == 10)   // \xd0\x9e\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd1\x8c\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8e\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f 1917 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\n                    \n                    ) {\n                        if (i == new Date().getDate() && D.getFullYear() == new Date().getFullYear() && D.getMonth() == new Date().getMonth()) {\n                            calendar += \'<td class="today holiday">\' + i;\n                        }else {\n                            calendar += \'<td class="holiday">\' + i;\n                        }\n                    }else if( // \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\n                    (i == 22 && D.getMonth() == 1) ||\n                    (i == 7 && D.getMonth() == 2) ||\n                    (i == 30 && D.getMonth() == 3) ||\n                    (i == 8 && D.getMonth() == 4) ||\n                    //(i == 1 && D.getMonth() == 8) ||\n                    (i == 6 && D.getMonth() == 10) ||\n                    (i == 31 && D.getMonth() == 11)\n                    ){\n                        if (i == new Date().getDate() && D.getFullYear() == new Date().getFullYear() && D.getMonth() == new Date().getMonth()) {\n                            calendar += \'<td class="today working shortDay">\' + i;\n                        }else {\n                            calendar += \'<td class="working shortDay">\' + i + \'<span class="holiday">*</span>\';\n                        }\n                    }else{\n                        if (i == new Date().getDate() && D.getFullYear() == new Date().getFullYear() && D.getMonth() == new Date().getMonth()) {\n                            calendar += \'<td class="today">\' + i;\n                        }else {\n                            calendar += \'<td>\' + i;\n                        }\n                    }\n\n                if (new Date(D.getFullYear(),D.getMonth(),i).getDay() == 0) {\n                    calendar += \'<tr>\';\n                }\n            }\n            for(var  i = DNlast; i < 7; i++) calendar += \'<td>&nbsp;\';\n            document.querySelector(\'#\'+id+\' tbody\').innerHTML = calendar;\n            g.value = D.getFullYear();\n            m.selected = true;\n            if (document.querySelectorAll(\'#\'+id+\' tbody tr\').length < 6) {\n                document.querySelector(\'#\'+id+\' tbody\').innerHTML += \'<tr><td>&nbsp;<td>&nbsp;<td>&nbsp;<td>&nbsp;<td>&nbsp;<td>&nbsp;<td>&nbsp;\';\n            }\n\n            //document.querySelector(\'#\'+id+\' option[value="\' + new Date().getMonth() + \'"]\').style.fontWeight = \'bold\'; // \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x83\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f\xd1\x86\n        }\n        var monthStart = 0;\n        if (new Date().getFullYear() != 2019)\n            monthStart = 0;\n        else monthStart = new Date().getMonth();\n\n        Calendar6("calendar6",2019, monthStart);\n        //Calendar4("calendar4",new Date().getFullYear(),new Date().getMonth());\n        document.querySelector(\'#calendar6\').onchange = function Kalendar4() {\n            Calendar6("calendar6",2019,parseFloat(document.querySelector(\'#calendar6 select\').options[document.querySelector(\'#calendar6 select\').selectedIndex].value));\n            //Calendar4("calendar4",document.querySelector(\'#calendar4 input\').value,parseFloat(document.querySelector(\'#calendar4 select\').options[document.querySelector(\'#calendar4 select\').selectedIndex].value));\n        }\n
          </script>
